< text>
A quaint little shop in a quaint little town. The fudge is made so that it will not melt, which is perfect since temperatures can be quite warm in So-Cal and you rarely just drive to Solvang to pick up fudge and leave. This allows you to meander through the streets without ending up with a puddle of sugar.

Fudge is sold here by the slice, not the square. (Side note: "slice" in this context sounds dainty and delicate. It is no more dainty and delicate than using a chainsaw to widdle.)  The price is very reasonable - $5 to $6 per slice. We sampled a couple before settling on Chocolate Orange. It's quite rich, but smooth as can be. A little goes a long way.<//text>

Before the hours reduction I was already having a hard time being able to get there after work and sometimes getting out of there late because I literally raced straight from work across town.
I was contacted by the district manager and immediately called her back to let her know I was very sorry for the times that I left late and understood her safety concerns. She in fact told me that she was surprised I called back and really appreciated my understanding and sincere apologies.
HOWEVER, She has been left multiple voicemails by myself as well as another individual and she has yet, after three months, to respond to any of them.

When I spoke to my husband he informed me that during his last phone call with the desk clerk, he had expressed that this was totally unacceptable for the hundreds of dollars that we‚Äôve been paying for over a year.

Her response?
Unfortunately there‚Äôs nothing that can be done in the name of customer service and that all tenants will have to keep paying full price even though access and service have all been slashed by more than half.

I have spoken with two of my neighboring tenants and the overall vibe is that everybody is really feeling slighted by this company. All the way from the higher ups plain ignoring phone calls down to the property manager acting like they have absolutely no clue when any of this ‚Äúconstruction‚Äù is slated to end.

And on a sidenote, Google maps is showing that from an aerial viewpoint all of the drive isles have been widened and all of the outer units have been installed to the point where it is visible without unsafe debris or work vehicles (For the longest time everything from an aerial point of view showed an absolute wreck).

My question is this.......
when did it become acceptable to treat current, loyal renters like yesterday‚Äôs news all in the name of the almighty dollar and the expectation of new renters who will take our units now that the company can force them to pay more?

I work in customer service for a living and it is really disheartening to see that this kind of easy come, easy go attitude is pervading not just the huge corporations but the smaller, more amiable and accessible business as well.

I guess I will have to start searching for a new location and company at a greater distance but I am more than willing to pay the extra dollars in gas, even suffer the inconvenience in distance, to get service that I can trust.
Especially during a time when so much is up in the air for our community and country.< /text><pics>None< /pics>< Resp>

This is my go to spot for bubble tea. The best part really is their hours, being able to get my tea fix until 11pm at night is pretty important to me lol.

The Boba is usually good, though they often run out. I've maybe only ever had 1 or 2 drinks where the Boba itself was off. The teas are good, but some aren't as good without the Boba, so if they've run out of Boba, select a drink that works without it.

They're very accommodating to diets as well and will customize the drink to your needs.

The limited edition drinks are typically very good. Their fruit drinks are great as well (very fresh).< /review>

Super chill atmosphere. Lots of space to sit or even lounge in couches. I can't speak on behalf of the food, but the drinks are absolutely incredible! They definitely have their own version of cocktails that I've never had before.

<user_id>108907257910820725065< /user_id>< Text>
White Horse is a really great place to visit for delicious New Orleans Cajun. The food and drinks are very well priced for the outstanding quality you get, and the servers and bartenders are extremely knowledgeable as well. Feel safe when visiting, everything is being done with the COVID best practice requirements. Great happy hour offerings as well, especially for those that like 'Old Fashioneds'. I really liked and appreciated the old school music and old fashioned dim bar surroundings, it really was refreshing. The dark wood and red upholstery The exterior design is very tasteful and catches your attention when passing by. The set up works great for those looking for a group setting or even just for couples. I found the brunch menu to be especially enticing, I'm going to need to come back a couple of times to try out all the things that looked promising. The parking structure is right next door for maximum convenience. This place is truly a hidden gem amongst all the other great places in Pasadena. I'm also looking forward to checking out their sister location, Craft Hill, which I've heard great things about. Brandon was an amazing team member and recommended the fried chicken sandwich, which was fantastic. He knew all the items on the menu almost from memory and went above and beyond to walk me through everything. I'm glad I went with his recommendations. He also told me some cool things to do in the area and South Pasadena, so I have those on my list as well. They don't skip on the portions either, you'll definitely satisfy your appetite and probably have some leftovers as well. I can't think of much they can do to improve things, everything was so great! I plan on visiting again sooner rather than later.</Text>

<gmapID>0x80c2c37131b91407:0x665921b8ebcce1a5< /gmapID>< Review>
I like to cook. I do. I really really do. So I already know when I go out to eat that I can prepare the meal I‚Äôm going to eat just as well as the restaurant for a fraction of the price. Therefore service, ambiance, and cleanliness are of the upmost importance to me.

Before I start with the bad I should really say that the food was outstanding. Very flavorful and well presented. The ambiance was relaxed making the White Horse seem like a popular place among the young and old alike. Cleanliness in the bar and restrooms was above average.

My only complaint was the attentiveness and speed of the staff.  Our drink orders took forever. Our food (two dishes) was delivered about fifteen minutes apart and it seems they really didn‚Äôt want to bring us the check.

Overall it was a good experience. However, with dozens and dozens of restaurants to choose from, owners/managers must strive for perfection in all aspects of their restaurant and not just the food. When it comes down to it, almost anyone can make a tuna sandwich and mix a drink.</Review>

<response>None< /response><gmap_id>0x80c2c37131b91407:0x665921b8ebcce1a5<//gmap_id><user_name>David Perez< /user_name></record></dataset><record>
< user_id>
102595820736418415381</user_id>
<username>James Wan</username><Date>1583312770688< /Date><Rating>2< /Rating>< text>
A packed dining room and bar put this place quite in the limelight as you enter on a weekend evening. Unfortunately, there were far too many misses to honestly click on an extra star for the rating.

The bar seriously needs to pay attention to customers. Waiting for my party and waiting at the bar, and trying to get a drink was an impossible 5 minutes. They were treating me like I just came out of an AA meeting.

The menu seems to hit most of the notes for a hungry patron. At first glance, you can see it is well designed. Something for everyone wraps the context of each category. Fine Wagyu meats, a great burger, your standard salmon dish, and an attractive Southern Fried Chicken.

Dig deeper and you can find the pretentiousness of certain items. The use of Wagyu in smoked brisket, for example, is quite a redundancy. Why pay for a Wagyu priced cut that is supposed to be slow-smoked/cooked?

The Jumbalaya Rissoto is in fact not "risotto," and made with orzo pasta. Granted it is stated in the description as orzo, the title is completely misleading. If a person was gluten intolerant this would be a horrific experience. This dish is totally not worthy of the $26 price tag for a pasta dish.

The service felt like the servers were really working hard. I overheard a waiter mumbling about covering 8 large tables. I commend the service timing for everyone at the table.

The drinks here are very good. The bar certainly displays some craft behind their creations. I would return for their happy hour, and possibly a revisit for a sample of other items.

I do miss Cheval Blanc that once took this location to new heights in french cuisine.<//text>

< review>
What a wonderful surprise!! The White Horse Lounge is a great place for family, out of town guest spot, romantic two or just friends! The food is an explosion of flavors and mouth watering treats! I kind you not.. the southern fried chicken is seasoned to delight, the Hoe cake made me moooan, the salmon avec haricot verts satisfies the palate with lightness.. and the drinks..well let's just say they don't hold back! The ambiance is Nu Oleans almost classic brothel style with elegant private cubbies tucked aside; it's warm and welcoming and smooth music playing in the background will catch you for a recognizable song.. the service is exceptional, making sure you're delighted to be there. The chef is to be applauded..my understanding is he's been there about a year and a half and he's for sure making a statement at the White Horse Lounge! Oh and did I mention the Blackberry peach cobbler!! The place is high on my list you won't be disappointed!!< /review>

Update:
We stopped by and has Arroyo hamburger which was fantastic. Big Josh, the chef stopped by and revealed that the every ingrediants used here is from a local and certified grower. We had Judy taken care of us.

Josh was proud of his cooking style learned from her Japanese granma.

A classy place with great selection and service. We just dropped in and got hooked.

We sat in and Cesar took our order. He suggested Strawberry Buck and Peach Schnapps to start with which were both sweet drinks and fit the occasion. Bertta, the manager stopped by and chatted with us over the specials for the night.

The Bread and Butter we got was warmly toasted with some  greens and slice of pork. We ordered Porklion and Arroyo Burger. Both were good and tasty. The portions were adequate.

We ended with Pear cobbler with scoop of ice cream. Well made and filling.< /Text>

< Review>
We came to White Horse Lounge in Pasadena to celebrate a friend's birthday.
Love the beautiful bar area. It‚Äôs got that classic American bar vibe.
Since we have a large party, we were seated in the private room in the back.
Very simple one page menu. They have quite a few small bites that are great with drinks.

Market Hummus | $10
House Lavash, EVOO, Fresh Garnish
We ordered a few appetizers to share.
Market Hummus was just ok. It lacked flavor.

Seared Brussel Sprouts | $10
Smoked Tomatoes, Basil, Parmesan
Seared Brussel Sprouts was great. We enjoyed the addition of tomatoes and basil.

Garlic Truffle Fries | $9
Truffle Oil, Parmesan, Gremolata
We love the Garlic Truffle Fries. Thick and crunchy fries seasoned with truffle oil and cheese.

Bone-In New York 22 oz | $45
For steak orders, guests can pick 2 sides and a sauce for the meat.
A friend ordered the huge Bone-In New York, and she almost finished it!
She likes the steak, but didn‚Äôt like the cajun butter sauce.

Ribeye 16 oz | $35
Dr. P and I both ordered the Ribeye.
The steak was cooked perfectly. Very delicious.
For sides, I got the twice baked potato and corn succotash.
I enjoyed both. And the horseradish sauce was great with the steak.

The Black Sea | $25
Squid Ink Tagliolini, Dinapoli Tomato, Calamari, Prawn, Fin√©s Herbes
A few people ordered The Black Sea ‚Äì the squid ink seafood pasta.
Everyone said it was way too salty, and nobody liked it.

I like that we had the private room, and could be as loud as we want.
Service could be better. Our waitress didn‚Äôt check on us often.
We had to go out to find her a few times.
It was a really fun night with friends.</Review>
